<script type="text/javascript">
	timeout = null;

	series = [];
	seriesContainer = document.getElementById('seriesContainer');
	seriesElements = seriesContainer.getElementsByTagName("a");
	seriesNum = seriesElements.length;

	for (var i = 0; i < seriesNum; ++i) {
		series.push(seriesElements[i].innerHTML);
	}

	document.getElementById('serForm').style.display = "block";

	function searchSeries() {
		var reg = new RegExp('(?:^|\\s)' + document.getElementById('serInput').value.replace(/[[\]{}()*+?.\\^$|]/g, '\\$&').replace(/&/g, '&amp;'), 'i');
		var num = 0;
		for (var i = 0; i < seriesNum; ++i) {
			if (reg.test(series[i])) {
				++num;
				seriesElements[i].innerHTML = series[i].replace(reg, '<strong>$&</strong>');
				seriesElements[i].parentNode.className = "";
				seriesElements[i].parentNode.style.display = 'block';
			} else {
				seriesElements[i].parentNode.className = "hidden";
				seriesElements[i].parentNode.style.display = 'none';
			}
		}

		$(".genre").each(function () {
			active = $("li:not(.hidden)", this).length;
			if (!active) {
				this.style.display = "none";
			} else {
				this.style.display = "block";
			}
		})
	}
